,You and your flock of sheep are wondering the feilds of Italy and see an abondon church, its sunset. Do you wish to rest for the night? [[Countinue]] [[Rest in Church]]You use your book as a pillow and slumber away. You have a dream that leaves you in a stir. When you wake your flock begins to scramble. [[gather the sheep to leave]] [[leave the sheep there and look for some food]]You countine to wonder till its nightfall. You dont have shelter to protect the sheep, you stay up all night to [[keep guard]]. [[Quit being a shepherd and be a preist]]You are heading to a merchant to sell wool. You speak to your sheep about the merchents daughter you met a year prior. [[You will arrive at the city in 3 days]] [[you are going crazy, leave the sheep and find a doctor]]You countinue to wonder the feilds for food and water.You arrive and the merchant askes you to wait till the afternoon. While you wait, you read and speak with the merchants daughter about her life in the village. She askes you why you became a shepered even though you can read. [[You brush off the question and speak of your exciting travels]] [[you say "becuase I want to"]]You are attracted to the girl and desire to stay in one place for the rest of his life [[The merchant is ready for you]] [[You ask for the girls hand]]Your shortness doesn't appeal to the girl but at this point in time, it doesn't really matter what woman think [[You ask for the girls hand]]The merchant appers and asks for the wool of four sheep and tells you to [[return the next year]]. [[ask him for a job]]Well you actully ask the merchant for the girls hand. He accepts, you sell your sheep and begin working with the merchant and will soon gain wealth.It is almost one year later, you are four days away from the merchent and sleep in the same church, has the same dream and thinks about the merchant's daughter. [[You countine on with your sheep and admire their simplicity]] [[you think of how dumb sheep are and decide to kill them all]]You recall telling your father you want to travel instead of being a preist. Your father doesnt think traveling will give you what you want but gives you three gold coins to buy sheep. You look at your sheep and think about their perspective. Do they like to travel and see new places everyday? You decide they only care about eating, and think about the collective single mindedness that the flock shares and compare it with your feelings for the merchants daughter. [[countinue.]] [[give up]]when you arrive in the town you recall an old woman who interprets dreams. [[forget about the dream and look for the merchants dautgher]] [[go to the old woman]]You found her! Go fall in love, have some kids, settle down. Become a wealthy merchant.Once you arrive the dream interpreter takes your hands and chants a Gypsy prayer. You get sacared and your hands tremble. You pull your hands away and tell the woman you dont want the reading anymore. The interpreter tells you she can help and she will still charge you if you leave early. [[You stay]] [[You leave]][[You explain your dream]]... you are in a field with your sheep when a child starts to play with them. The child grabs your hands, transports you to the pyramids in Egypt, and tells you that you will find a treasure near them. As the child begins to say the exact location of treasure, you wake up. The old woman charges you a pretty penny and you do on your way. [[find something else to do]]The woman tells you she will not charge you but askes for 10 percent of the treasure. You laugh and agree. She insist that you go to the pyramids to find the treasure. [[You leave disappointed]] but atlease you didn't get charged!You get some food and a new book and sit in town. While you are reading an old Arab approches you. You ignore the man at first but he wont leave you alone. [[ignore him]] [[talk to him]]that was a bit rude but you can just [[find something else to do]] The old man questions you about your book. The old man says it like most other books that make people beleive the worlds biggest lie, that nobody can choose their own fate, or personal legend. You say well you controlled your fate by becoming a shepherd instead of a preist. [[The man then introduced himself as]]Melchizedek, the King of Salem. You think this man is crazy, you never heard of Salem. The man tells you, if you give him a tenth of your sheep he will tell you how to find your treasure. You think the old man works with the gypsy becuase you didnt mention the treasure. But the old man then writes your parents names in the sand, things him nor the gypsy would know. [[this is creepy, leave]] [[countinue to speak with him]]That was super creepy! Go see your sheep, they will make you feel better! [[See sheep]]Melchizedek explains a personal legend is what that person most desires to accomplish in their life.Everyone knows their personal legend when they are young and as they grow older, they grow to feel they can never achieve it. The man says he appears to people that are about to give up on their personal legends as a solution or idea, he tells you he will help you if you give him one tenth of your flock.
